width=\"99%\"><tbody><tr><td><div class=\"story\"><div><a href=\"/node/3986490\"><span class=\"storytitle\">[slides] #WebRTC for the #IoT | @CloudExpo @MontesLu #M2M #AI #Telecom</span></a></div><div class=\"storyauthor\">By Elizabeth White</div><div class=\"storysummary\"><img src=\"http://res.cdn.sys-con.com/story/jan17/3986490/Luis%20Montes%20468%202.png\" align=\"left\" border=\"0\" </tr>\n</tbody></table>\n<img src=\"http://www2.sys-con.com/eventserver/general/cloudeast2010/skin/blank.gif\" width=\"15\" height=\"15\" border=\"0\"><br>  \n</div>\n<div><div class=\"portlettitlesmall\">@CloudExpo Blogs</div><table border=\"0\" cellpadding=\"2\" cellspacing=\"0\" width=\"99%\"><tbody><tr><td><div class=\"story\"><div><a href=\"/node/4003542\"><span class=\"storytitle\">FutureScape: Worldwide Cloud in 2017 and 2018</span></a></div><div class=\"storyauthor\">By Antonella Corno</div><div class=\"storysummary\"><img src=\"http://res.cdn.sys-con.com/story/feb17/4003542/Learning%20at%20Cisco%20468.png\" align=\"left\" border=\"0\" hspace=\"2\" vspace=\"2\" width=\"90\" height=\"51\" alt=\"\">Cloud usage continues to gain momentum across all industries.
